/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18A тАФ SESSION & CASE-SAVE RULES (OFFICIAL VERSION)
 * Applies To:
 *    - Utils.gs (Session Engine + Case Engine)
 *    - Flows.gs (Step transitions)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *   Define official rules for saving sessions, saving cases,
 *   and when full session resets must occur.
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ SESSION INITIALIZATION RULES
 ************************************************************
 * A new session is created when:
 *   - No existing active session for this WhatsApp number
 *   - OR previous session was reset after case completion
 *   - OR eligibility rejection тЖТ user selected "No"
 *
 * New session template:
 *   Current_Step_Code = "LANG_SELECT"
 *   Region_Group      = detectRegionByPhone()
 *   Preferred_Language = ""
 *   Flow_Type          = ""
 *   Temp_Data_Json     = "{}"
 *   Updated_At         = NOW
 *
 * тЖТ MUST be saved immediately.
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ SESSION SAVE RULES (WHEN TO SAVE)
 ************************************************************
 * ALWAYS save session whenever:
 *
 *   тЬФ The bot moves to a new step
 *       e.g., LANG_SELECT тЖТ USER_TYPE
 *             USER_TYPE тЖТ STEP_3A / STEP_3B / STEP_3C
 *             Qn тЖТ Qn+1
 *
 *   тЬФ After selecting preferred language
 *   тЬФ After selecting Flow Type (A/B/C)
 *   тЬФ After every answer to Q1тАУQn
 *   тЬФ After every media upload (photo/video)
 *   тЬФ After sending a session-timeout reminder
 *
 * Required:
 *   session.Updated_At = NOW
 *   Session.save()
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ SESSION TIMESTAMP RULES
 ************************************************************
 * On EVERY incoming message:
 *   session.Updated_At = NOW
 *   Session.save()
 *
 * Ensures accurate timeout detection.
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ SESSION RESET RULES (WHEN TO CLEAR SESSION)
 ************************************************************
 * A session must be fully deleted ONLY when:
 *
 *   тЬФ After successful case submission (STEP 4 тЖТ STEP 5)
 *   тЬФ After eligibility rejection AND user selects "No"
 *   тЬФ When user selects "Submit a new case" from Existing Case Menu
 *   тЬФ When user replies "0" in selection menus (partial reset only)
 *
 * In all other cases:
 *   тЖТ Session must remain active.
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ CASE CREATION RULES
 ************************************************************
 * Create a new row in Cases sheet ONLY when:
 *
 *   Flow A:
 *       Eligibility == "NO"
 *       AND Q1 тЖТ Q9 completed
 *
 *   Flow B:
 *       Q1 тЖТ Q11 completed
 *
 *   Flow C:
 *       Access Option 1 or 3 selected
 *       AND Q1 тЖТ Q15 completed
 *
 * After completion:
 *   Generate Case_ID
 *   Write to Cases sheet
 *   session.status = "CASE_SUBMITTED"
 *   Session.save()
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ CASE WRITE RULES
 ************************************************************
 * New case row MUST contain:
 *   - Case_ID
 *   - Created_At
 *   - WhatsApp_Number
 *   - Region
 *   - Language
 *   - Flow_Type
 *   - Q1тАжQn answers
 *   - Extra_Notes
 *   - Media_Links
 *   - Case_Status = "Submitted"
 *
 * All answers pulled from:
 *   session.Temp[key]
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ CASE UPDATE RULES (Case_Updates Sheet)
 ************************************************************
 * New update row created when:
 *   - Add new info
 *   - Upload media
 *   - Mark case as resolved
 *
 * Update row fields:
 *   Update_ID
 *   Case_ID
 *   Created_At
 *   Update_Type
 *   Content
 *   Media_Links
 *   Raw_JSON
 *
 * After update:
 *   Save update
 *   Send confirmation
 *   Send closing message
 *   Delete session
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ MEDIA SAVE RULES
 ************************************************************
 * Whenever image/video received:
 *   - Download from WhatsApp URL
 *   - Upload to Drive
 *   - Save Drive file ID in session.Temp
 *   - Session.save()
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ EXISTING CASE DETECTION RULES
 ************************************************************
 * Before starting STEP 2:
 *
 *   IF Cases.exists(WhatsApp_Number):
 *       session.Current_Step_Code = "EXISTING_CASE_MENU"
 *       Session.save()
 *       тЖТ Show menu
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ SESSION SAFETY (STATE MACHINE)
 ************************************************************
 * Rules:
 *   - Never skip steps
 *   - Never create case early
 *   - Always resume from session.Current_Step_Code
 *   - Reset ONLY when rules allow
 ************************************************************/


/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ FINAL RESET RULES
 ************************************************************
 * Session is FULLY cleared only:
 *   - After case submission
 *   - After rejection flow if user selects "No"
 *   - After update flow completion
 *
 * All other scenarios:
 *   тЖТ Keep session active.
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18B тАФ COMPLETE REJECTION SYSTEM (OFFICIAL VERSION)
 * Applies To:
 *    - Flows.gs (Router Logic)
 *    - Texts_Eligibility.gs (Rejection Messages)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *   Unified rejection logic for:
 *      1) Police/Agency Arrest Case (Flow A Eligibility = YES)
 *      2) No-Access Case (Flow C Source Option = 2)
 *
 *   Both must follow identical handling rules:
 *      тЖТ Send EXACT region-language rejection message
 *      тЖТ Offer: тАЬWould you like to submit a new case?тАЭ
 *      тЖТ If user selects 1 (Yes) тЖТ Reset тЖТ Go to STEP 2
 *      тЖТ If user selects 2 (No) тЖТ Send Closing Message тЖТ Reset session
 ************************************************************/

 *   - Send region-language rejection message (exact text)
 *   - Then show Post-Rejection Prompt:
 *         тАЬWould you like to submit a new case?тАЭ
 ************************************************************/

/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ ROUTER LOGIC SUMMARY (DO NOT MODIFY)
 ************************************************************
 *
 * IF (Flow A Eligibility == YES):
 *     sendPoliceRejection(session)
 *     askSubmitNewCase()
 *
 * IF (Flow C Access Option == "2"):
 *     sendNoAccessRejection(session)
 *     askSubmitNewCase()
 *
 * IF user selects "1":
 *     reset session (partial)
 *     go to STEP 2
 *
 * IF user selects "2":
 *     sendFinalClosingMessage()
 *     delete session
 *     end chat
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18C тАФ MEDIA & AUDIO HANDLING RULES (FINAL)
 * Applies To:
 *    - Utils.gs  (Media Download + Drive Upload Engine)
 *    - Flows.gs  (Media assignment per question)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *   Define the complete, official multimedia rules:
 *      тЬФ Media detection
 *      тЬФ Image/video download from WhatsApp
 *      тЬФ Upload to Google Drive
 *      тЬФ Store Drive file IDs inside session.Temp or Case_Updates
 *      тЬФ Multi-media (multiple images) support
 *      тЬФ Ear-friendly handling for photo-required steps
 *      тЬФ Voice/audio-only rules
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ MEDIA DETECTION RULES
 ************************************************************
 * On every incoming message, Flows.gs MUST detect:
 *
 *   - incomingText   (text cleaned/trimmed)
 *   - mediaUrl       (URL from WhatsApp payload)
 *   - mediaMime      (MIME type from WhatsApp payload)
 *   - mediaType      derived from MIME:
 *
 *       IF mediaMime startsWith("image/")  тЖТ IMAGE
 *       IF mediaMime startsWith("video/")  тЖТ VIDEO
 *       IF mediaMime startsWith("audio/")  тЖТ AUDIO
 *       ELSE                               тЖТ NONE
 *
 * If mediaUrl exists, treat message as media message first.
 *
 * NOTE:
 *   Media must ALWAYS be processed FIRST before checking text.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ IMAGE ACCEPTANCE RULES
 ************************************************************
 * If question requires a photo:
 *     (e.g., Flow A Q9, Flow B Q11, Flow C Q15)
 *
 *   тЬФ If mediaMime startsWith("image/"):
 *        тЖТ Accept
 *        тЖТ Download from WhatsApp
 *        тЖТ Upload to Drive
 *        тЖТ Save Drive file ID in session.Temp
 *
 *   тЬФ If user replies тАЬNoтАЭ or equivalent:
 *        тЖТ Accept as тАЬNo Image ProvidedтАЭ
 *
 *   тЬЦ If mediaMime is NOT image:
 *        тЖТ MUST send Texts.sendPhotoRequired(session)
 *        тЖТ Repeat same question
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ VIDEO HANDLING RULES
 ************************************************************
 * Videos are optional media for:
 *   - Update Case Flow (Upload photos/videos)
 *
 * Rules:
 *   тЬФ If mediaMime startsWith("video/"):
 *         тЖТ Download from WhatsApp
 *         тЖТ Upload to Drive
 *         тЖТ Store file ID inside:
 *             session.Temp.media_list OR Case_Updates.Media_Links
 *
 *   тЬФ Videos are NEVER acceptable where a photo is REQUIRED.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ AUDIO / VOICE NOTE HANDLING RULES
 ************************************************************
 * Audio messages fall under:
 *   - Voice-note allowed steps (general Q1тАУQn)
 *   - Text-only required steps тЖТ MUST reject
 *
 * RULE:
 *   If step_requires_text_only == true
 *   AND mediaMime startsWith("audio/"):
 *       тЖТ return Texts.sendVoiceNotAllowed(session)
 *       тЖТ Repeat same question
 *
 * Otherwise (text not strictly required):
 *   тЬФ Accept audio as valid answer
 *   тЬФ Transcribe? (No тАФ store raw audio reference only)
 *   тЬФ Upload audio to Drive
 *   тЬФ Save its file ID in session.Temp
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ DOWNLOAD FROM WHATSAPP (Utils.gs)
 ************************************************************
 * REQUIRED PROCESS:
 *
 *   function downloadMedia(mediaUrl, mimeType) {
 *       1. Fetch binary from mediaUrl using WhatsApp token
 *       2. Convert to Blob
 *       3. Return blob for upload
 *   }
 *
 * WhatsApp fetch headers:
 *   - Authorization: "Bearer " + WHATSAPP_TOKEN
 *   - Method: GET
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ GOOGLE DRIVE UPLOAD (Utils.gs)
 ************************************************************
 * REQUIRED PROCESS:
 *
 *   function uploadToDrive(blob, filename) {
 *       1. Select Drive folder (configured in CONF)
 *       2. folder.createFile(blob).setName(filename)
 *       3. Return Drive file ID
 *   }
 *
 * File naming:
 *   CASE-ID + "_Qn_" + timestamp
 *
 * All uploaded files must be:
 *   - Non-public
 *   - Stored in designated media folder
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ MULTI-MEDIA SUPPORT (MULTIPLE IMAGES)
 ************************************************************
 * Some questions must support multiple media messages:
 *
 *   - Flow A: Q9 (Optional)
 *   - Flow B: Q11 (Then & Now) тЖТ Allow 2+ photos
 *   - Flow C: Q15 (Then & Now) тЖТ Allow 2+ photos
 *   - Update Case Flow тЖТ Upload photos/videos
 *
 * Implementation pattern:
 *
 *   IF session.Temp.media_list does NOT exist:
 *       session.Temp.media_list = []
 *
 *   On each accepted media (image/video/audio):
 *       session.Temp.media_list.push(DriveFileID)
 *       Session.save()
 *
 * This ensures user can send:
 *   - Multiple images one by one
 *   - Image + video combinations (in update flow)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ ASSIGNING MEDIA TO QUESTIONS (Flows.gs)
 ************************************************************
 * After Drive upload:
 *
 *   If inside a question-step:
 *       session.Temp["Qn_media"] = DriveFileID
 *       OR append to media_list if multiple allowed
 *
 * MUST call Session.save() immediately.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ PHOTO REQUIRED LOGIC
 ************************************************************
 * EXACT TEXT from flow:
 *
 * If step_requires_photo == true
 * AND:
 *     - mediaUrl == null
 *     OR
 *     - mediaMime does NOT startWith("image/")
 *
 * THEN:
 *     return Texts.sendPhotoRequired(session)
 *
 * тЖТ Repeat same question without advancing step.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ VOICE-NOTE NOT ALLOWED LOGIC
 ************************************************************
 * EXACT TEXT from flow:
 *
 * If question_requires_text_only == true
 * AND mediaMime startsWith("audio/"):
 *     return Texts.sendVoiceNotAllowed(session)
 *
 * тЖТ Repeat same question
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ GENERAL MEDIA STORAGE (Case Creation)
 ************************************************************
 * For Flow A, B, C final case creation:
 *
 *   - All photo/video/audio file IDs MUST be written into:
 *       Cases.Media_Links
 *
 *   - If multiple:
 *       Join with commas OR structured JSON (developer choice)
 *
 *   - No modifications to images
 *   - Keep full file ID list
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 12 тАФ MEDIA STORAGE FOR CASE UPDATES
 ************************************************************
 * In Case_Updates sheet:
 *
 *   - Every new media message creates an update entry
 *   - Update_Type = "MEDIA"
 *   - Media_Links = file ID(s)
 *
 * After saving update:
 *     - Send confirmation
 *     - Send closing message
 *     - Reset session
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 13 тАФ NON-MEDIA TEXT RESPONSE WHILE PHOTO REQUIRED
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends text like:
 *     - тАЬokтАЭ
 *     - тАЬnoтАЭ
 *     - any text BUT photo required
 *
 * Allowed only if:
 *     - Flow explicitly says тАЬIf you donтАЩt have a photo, reply NoтАЭ
 *
 * Otherwise тЖТ MUST trigger:
 *     Texts.sendPhotoRequired(session)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 14 тАФ FALLBACK SAFETY RULE
 ************************************************************
 * If mediaMime is undefined or malformed:
 *     Treat as TEXT-only message.
 *
 * If mediaUrl exists but mediaMime missing:
 *     Reject unless image/video/audio requirement waived.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 15 тАФ SESSION SAVE AFTER MEDIA
 ************************************************************
 * After EVERY media upload:
 *
 *   - Update session.Temp
 *   - session.Updated_At = NOW
 *   - Session.save()
 *
 * Required so multiple media can be received back-to-back.
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18D тАФ MASTER LANGUAGE RENDERING RULES (OFFICIAL)
 * Applies To:
 *    - Texts_Wrapper.gs (all send functions)
 *    - Texts_*.gs       (multi-language message sets)
 *    - Flows.gs         (ensuring correct language output)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *   Enforce strict, consistent language behavior so that
 *   EVERY message is delivered ONLY in the userтАЩs selected
 *   Preferred_Language тАФ never mixed, never combined.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ LANGUAGE SELECTION IS FINAL FOR ENTIRE SESSION
 ************************************************************
 * After STEP 1 (LANG_SELECT):
 *
 *     session.Preferred_Language = "EN" | "UR" | "RUR"
 *                                 | "HI" | "BN" | "AR"
 *
 * RULE:
 *   Once selected, the language MUST be used for:
 *     - All menus
 *     - All questions (Q1тАУQn)
 *     - All rejection messages
 *     - All closing messages
 *     - All error/invalid messages
 *     - All system prompts
 *
 * Language must NEVER switch automatically.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ SINGLE-LANGUAGE OUTPUT RULE
 ************************************************************
 * For every Texts.send*() call:
 *
 *   The message MUST be returned in ONE language only:
 *
 *       Texts[lang].someMessage()
 *
 * There must NEVER be:
 *   - Combined EN+UR output
 *   - Multi-language mixes
 *   - Region menu fallback combos
 *
 * ONE message тЖТ ONE language block.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ HOW TO RENDER TEXT (Text Wrapper Logic)
 ************************************************************
 * Wrapper must:
 *
 *   function sendText(session, msgSet) {
 *        const lang = session.Preferred_Language;
 *        const body = msgSet[lang];
 *        return sendWhatsAppMessage(session.WhatsApp_Number, body);
 *   }
 *
 * RULE:
 *   - msgSet MUST contain EXACT TEXT for selected language
 *   - msgSet keys must match language codes
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ LANGUAGE CODES (MUST MATCH EXACTLY)
 ************************************************************
 *   "EN"  тЖТ English
 *   "UR"  тЖТ Urdu
 *   "RUR" тЖТ Roman Urdu
 *   "HI"  тЖТ Hindi
 *   "BN"  тЖТ Bangla
 *   "AR"  тЖТ Arabic
 *
 * No other codes may be used.
 * No auto-detection after STEP 1.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ REGION DOES NOT AFFECT MESSAGES (AFTER STEP 1)
 ************************************************************
 * Region detection affects:
 *     - The LANGUAGE MENU only
 *     - The USER TYPE MENU variations
 *
 * AFTER Preferred_Language is selected:
 *     REGION MUST NOT influence text selection.
 *
 * Examples:
 *     - A PK user selecting English тЖТ Receives EN messages only.
 *     - An IN user selecting Urdu   тЖТ Receives UR messages only.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ RULE FOR ERROR / VALIDATION MESSAGES
 ************************************************************
 * INVALID OPTION:
 *     Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *
 * INVALID TEXT:
 *     Texts.sendInvalidText(session, question)
 *
 * PHOTO REQUIRED:
 *     Texts.sendPhotoRequired(session)
 *
 * VOICE NOT ALLOWED:
 *     Texts.sendVoiceNotAllowed(session)
 *
 * UNEXPECTED KEYWORD:
 *     Texts.sendUnexpectedKeywordReminder(session)
 *
 * SESSION TIMEOUT:
 *     Texts.sendSessionExpiredReminder(session)
 *
 * ALL must use ONLY:
 *     session.Preferred_Language
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ WHEN LANGUAGE MUST NOT CHANGE
 ************************************************************
 * These events may NOT change language:
 *
 *   - Case submission
 *   - Case update
 *   - Rejection flow
 *   - Existing case menu
 *   - Returning after inactivity
 *   - Sending any error/invalid message
 *
 * ONLY STEP 1 may set language.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ CONTENT RETRIEVAL MUST MATCH EXACT TEXT IN FLOW FILE
 ************************************************************
 * For every message type, wrapper must retrieve:
 *
 *     EXACT text defined in Full n Final Flow Updated.txt
 *
 * No rewrite.
 * No trimming.
 * No paraphrasing.
 * No automatic punctuation changes.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ TEXTS MUST BE ISOLATED BY LANGUAGE
 ************************************************************
 * Structure:
 *
 *   const Texts = {
 *        EN: { ... },
 *        UR: { ... },
 *        RUR: { ... },
 *        HI: { ... },
 *        BN: { ... },
 *        AR: { ... }
 *   };
 *
 * Each object MUST contain:
 *    - The EXACT wording for its language block
 *    - No duplicate languages inside other blocks
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ SYSTEM MUST IGNORE USER LANGUAGE MESSAGES
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends:
 *   - "english"
 *   - "urdu"
 *   - "arabic"
 *   - "change language"
 *
 * AFTER Step 1 тЖТ MUST NOT switch language.
 *
 * Instead:
 *   тЖТ Continue flow using the stored Preferred_Language.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ SENDING PROMPTS IN FLOWS.GS
 ************************************************************
 * For any step, Flows.gs must do:
 *
 *   const msg = Texts[session.Preferred_Language].StepQ1;
 *   return Texts.send(session.WhatsApp_Number, msg);
 *
 * No conditional branching by region after Step 1.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 12 тАФ LANGUAGE LOCK RULE (MANDATORY)
 ************************************************************
 * From Step 2 onward:
 *
 *   The system is "language-locked".
 *
 * LOCK stays until:
 *   - Case is submitted тЖТ Session reset
 *   - User exits via rejection тЖТ Session reset
 *
 * New sessions always begin with:
 *   LANG_SELECT
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18E тАФ REGION-BASED LANGUAGE FALLBACK RULES (OFFICIAL)
 *
 * Applies To:
 *    - Utils.gs              (Region detection)
 *    - Texts_LangMenus.gs    (Language Menu rendering)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *    Define EXACT mapping of:
 *       REGION тЖТ Allowed Languages
 *
 *    These rules ONLY apply during STEP 1 (LANG_SELECT).
 *    AFTER language is selected, region plays NO role.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ REGION DETECTION VALUES (Utils.gs)
 ************************************************************
 * detectRegionByPhone(number) MUST return EXACTLY:
 *
 *   "PK"   тЖТ Pakistan
 *   "IN"   тЖТ India
 *   "BD"   тЖТ Bangladesh
 *   "ME"   тЖТ Middle East (GCC: +966, +971, +973, +974, +968, +965)
 *   "OTHER"
 *
 * No other codes allowed.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ ALLOWED LANGUAGES PER REGION (STRICT)
 ************************************************************
 * During STEP 1 (LANG_SELECT), bot MUST show ONLY the languages
 * allowed for that region.
 *
 * NO deviations.
 * NO merged regions.
 * NO auto-expansion.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2A тАФ PAKISTAN (PK)
 ************************************************************
 * Allowed Languages:
 *
 *   1я╕ПтГг Urdu (UR)
 *   2я╕ПтГг Roman Urdu (RUR)
 *   3я╕ПтГг English (EN)
 *
 * These must always appear in this order.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2B тАФ INDIA (IN)
 ************************************************************
 * Allowed Languages:
 *
 *   1я╕ПтГг Hindi (HI)
 *   2я╕ПтГг Urdu (UR)
 *   3я╕ПтГг Roman Urdu (RUR)
 *   4я╕ПтГг English (EN)
 *
 * EXACT order must be preserved.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2C тАФ BANGLADESH (BD)
 ************************************************************
 * Allowed Languages:
 *
 *   1я╕ПтГг Bangla (BN)
 *   2я╕ПтГг English (EN)
 *
 * No Urdu/Hindi options.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2D тАФ MIDDLE EAST (ME)
 ************************************************************
 * Allowed Languages:
 *
 *   1я╕ПтГг Arabic (AR)
 *   2я╕ПтГг English (EN)
 *   3я╕ПтГг Urdu (UR)
 *   4я╕ПтГг Roman Urdu (RUR)
 *
 * EXACT order required.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2E тАФ OTHER REGIONS (OTHER)
 ************************************************************
 * Allowed Languages:
 *
 *   1я╕ПтГг English (EN)
 *   2я╕ПтГг Urdu (UR)
 *   3я╕ПтГг Roman Urdu (RUR)
 *
 * No Bangla, Hindi, or Arabic outside home regions.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ MENU RENDERING RULES
 ************************************************************
 * Texts_LangMenus.gs MUST:
 *
 *   - Select menu based on region
 *   - Use ONLY the languages mapped above
 *   - Use EXACT text for each language option
 *   - Maintain EXACT numbering for options
 *
 * Region тЖТ Menu (EXAMPLE STRUCTURE):
 *
 *   const LangMenus = {
 *       PK:   Texts.EN_LangMenu_PK,      // 3 options
 *       IN:   Texts.EN_LangMenu_IN,      // 4 options
 *       BD:   Texts.EN_LangMenu_BD,      // 2 options
 *       ME:   Texts.EN_LangMenu_ME,      // 4 options
 *       OTHER:Texts.EN_LangMenu_OTHER    // 3 options
 *   };
 *
 * IMPORTANT:
 *   Menu text MUST match Full n Final Flow Updated.txt exactly.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ FALLBACK LOGIC WHEN USER SENDS INVALID LANGUAGE OPTION
 ************************************************************
 * If user selects a number NOT in allowed range:
 *
 *   тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *   тЖТ Repeat LANGUAGE MENU for that region
 *
 * Do NOT switch region during fallback.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ LANGUAGE LOCK AFTER SELECTION
 ************************************************************
 * Once user selects language:
 *
 *     session.Preferred_Language = chosen_code
 *
 * After this:
 *
 *     Region MUST NOT override language.
 *
 * Language remains locked for entire session.
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18F тАФ STATE MACHINE SAFETY RULES (OFFICIAL VERSION)
 *
 * Applies To:
 *    - Flows.gs (Main Router)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *    Prevent:
 *       - Wrong step jumps
 *       - Flow corruption
 *       - Lost sessions
 *       - Out-of-order question transitions
 *
 *    And enforce:
 *       - Auto-repair (restore previous correct step)
 *       - Hard protection of flow sequence
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ MASTER RULE: NEVER JUMP STEPS
 ************************************************************
 * The router must NEVER:
 *     - Skip a step
 *     - Jump ahead
 *     - Jump backwards (unless repair logic triggers)
 *     - Move into a step that does not follow the current one
 *
 * Allowed transitions MUST match EXACT flow sequence:
 *
 *   LANG_SELECT тЖТ USER_TYPE
 *   USER_TYPE тЖТ 3A_xx / 3B_xx / 3C_xx
 *
 *   Q1 тЖТ Q2
 *   Q2 тЖТ Q3
 *   ...
 *
 * NO dynamic routing.
 * NO shortcuts.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ ROUTER VALIDATION BEFORE PROCESSING
 ************************************************************
 * On every incoming message:
 *
 *   - Load session
 *   - Validate:
 *        session.Flow_Type
 *        session.Current_Step_Code
 *        session.Preferred_Language (after Step 1)
 *
 * If ANY of these missing:
 *     тЖТ Auto-repair:
 *         session.Current_Step_Code = "LANG_SELECT"
 *         Session.save()
 *         return Texts.sendLanguageMenu(session)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ HARD BLOCK: NO STEP UNTIL LANGUAGE IS SELECTED
 ************************************************************
 * If session.Preferred_Language is empty
 * AND session.Current_Step_Code != "LANG_SELECT":
 *
 *     тЖТ Auto-fix:
 *          session.Current_Step_Code = "LANG_SELECT"
 *          Session.save()
 *          return Texts.sendLanguageMenu(session)
 *
 * This prevents broken sessions from jumping ahead.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ FLOW TYPE CONSISTENCY PROTECTION
 ************************************************************
 * After user chooses Flow A / B / C:
 *
 *     session.Flow_Type MUST NOT change.
 *
 * If system detects:
 *     - Missing Flow_Type
 *     - Unexpected Flow_Type
 *     - Wrong Flow_Type for the current step
 *
 * Then auto-repair:
 *
 *     session.Current_Step_Code = "USER_TYPE"
 *     session.Flow_Type = ""
 *     Session.save()
 *     return Texts.sendUserTypeMenu(session)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ STEP REPAIR RULE (AUTO-REBUILD)
 ************************************************************
 * If incomingText does NOT match expected pattern for step:
 *
 *     тЖТ DO NOT advance step
 *     тЖТ DO NOT break session
 *
 * Instead:
 *     тЖТ Repeat same question using language-locked Texts[]
 *
 * Example:
 *   - User sends letters for a numeric-only step
 *   - User sends emoji for a Yes/No step
 *
 * System ALWAYS replays the same question.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ OUT-OF-ORDER MESSAGE PROTECTION
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends a message for:
 *     - a previous question
 *     - a future question
 *     - an unrelated response
 *
 * Then:
 *     тЖТ Ignore the incorrect input
 *     тЖТ Replay the current step EXACTLY
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ INVALID KEYWORD PROTECTION
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends:
 *     - HELP
 *     - MENU
 *     - HELLO
 *     - SALAM
 *     - RANDOM WORDS
 *
 * During any question step:
 *
 *     тЖТ Do NOT change step
 *     тЖТ Do NOT leave flow
 *
 *     тЖТ Must send:
 *           Texts.sendUnexpectedKeywordReminder(session)
 *
 *     тЖТ Repeat same question
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ MEDIA MIS-MATCH PROTECTION
 ************************************************************
 * If step requires:
 *
 *     - TEXT only тЖТ audio not allowed
 *     - PHOTO only тЖТ reject text/audio/non-image media
 *
 * Then:
 *     тЖТ Send EXACT validation message
 *     тЖТ Stay on SAME step (no advancement)
 *
 * System MUST NOT:
 *     - Mark question complete
 *     - Proceed to next step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ CASE SUBMISSION STAGE SAFETY
 ************************************************************
 * At final step (Step 4 тЖТ Step 5):
 *
 *   If any required Qn missing:
 *       тЖТ Do NOT submit case
 *       тЖТ DO NOT reset
 *       тЖТ Rewind automatically to first missing Qn
 *
 * Auto-repair:
 *       session.Current_Step_Code = first_incomplete_Qn
 *       Session.save()
 *       return Texts.sendQn(session)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ EXISTING CASE MENU SAFETY
 ************************************************************
 * If user enters:
 *     - тАЬUpdate CaseтАЭ
 *     - тАЬView StatusтАЭ
 *     - тАЬSubmit New CaseтАЭ
 *
 * While router expects a QUESTION step:
 *
 *     тЖТ MUST ignore
 *     тЖТ Replay the current Qn
 *
 * Existing Case Menu ONLY allowed during its specific state.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ POST-REJECTION SAFETY
 ************************************************************
 * After ANY rejection (Flow A police/agency OR Flow C no-access):
 *
 *   The ONLY valid inputs:
 *       1 тЖТ New Case
 *       2 тЖТ End Chat
 *
 * ANY other input:
 *       тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *       тЖТ Repeat SAME two options
 *
 * No escape allowed.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 12 тАФ INACTIVITY REPAIR RULE
 ************************************************************
 * If user returns after timeout:
 *
 *   тЖТ MUST resend last question EXACTLY
 *   тЖТ MUST NOT jump ahead
 *
 * System uses:
 *     Texts.sendSessionExpiredReminder(session)
 *
 * Then repeats SAME step based on session.Current_Step_Code.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 13 тАФ FINAL PROTECTION RULE
 ************************************************************
 * The router MUST obey:
 *
 *     session.Current_Step_Code
 *
 * as the SINGLE source of truth.
 *
 * System MUST NOT:
 *     - Infer next steps from user messages
 *     - Guess missing values
 *     - Jump ahead based on content
 *
 * ALL control belongs to:
 *
 *     STEP тЖТ Qn тЖТ Qn+1
 *
 * EXACT order from the master flow.
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18G тАФ ERROR & EDGE-CASE HANDLING (FINAL + OFFICIAL)
 *
 * Applies To:
 *    - Flows.gs (Input validation & error routing)
 *    - Utils.gs  (Validation helpers)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *    Define EXACT rules for:
 *       - Handling invalid answers
 *       - Preventing flow breaks
 *       - Managing random inputs/emojis
 *       - Validation for each step type
 *       - Full recovery without losing progress
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ INVALID OPTION (NUMERIC MENUS)
 ************************************************************
 * If step expects a numeric menu option (1, 2, 3тАж):
 *
 *   If incomingText NOT in allowed options:
 *       тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *       тЖТ Repeat same step
 *
 * Examples of invalid inputs:
 *   - alphabetic ("a", "yes", "hello")
 *   - emojis ("ЁЯШВ", "тЭдя╕П", "ЁЯСН")
 *   - random digits ("9", "777", "12")
 *   - blank messages
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ INVALID YES/NO ANSWERS
 ************************************************************
 * If step expects:
 *      1я╕ПтГг Yes
 *      2я╕ПтГг No
 *
 * And user sends ANYTHING ELSE:
 *
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat same step
 *
 * Letters, words, emojis, mixed text тЖТ ALWAYS invalid.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ TEXT-ONLY QUESTIONS (NO MEDIA, NO AUDIO)
 ************************************************************
 * Some questions require STRICT text-only answers.
 * Example:
 *   - Name
 *   - Address
 *   - Relation to missing person
 *
 * If user sends:
 *     - Audio
 *     - Video
 *     - Image
 *
 * THEN:
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendVoiceNotAllowed(session)  (for audio)
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendPhotoNotAllowed(session)  (if applicable)
 *     тЖТ Repeat same step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ PHOTO-REQUIRED QUESTIONS
 ************************************************************
 * If step requires a PHOTO:
 *
 *   If user sends:
 *       - text only
 *       - audio
 *       - non-image file
 *
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendPhotoRequired(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat same step
 *
 * User may reply тАЬNoтАЭ ONLY when allowed by flow.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ EMOJI / SYMBOL / SPECIAL CHAR HANDLING
 ************************************************************
 * If input contains ONLY emojis or symbols:
 *       тЖТ INVALID
 *
 * If input contains mixed characters:
 *       тАЬhello ЁЯШВтАЭ
 *
 *   Then treat as text and apply step-specific validation:
 *
 *       If numeric expected тЖТ INVALID
 *       If yes/no expected  тЖТ INVALID
 *       If free-text allowed тЖТ ACCEPT
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ RANDOM WORDS OR IRRELEVANT TEXT
 ************************************************************
 * If user replies with unrelated words:
 *     тАЬokтАЭ
 *     тАЬhaanтАЭ
 *     тАЬplease helpтАЭ
 *     тАЬmissingтАЭ
 *     тАЬbhaiтАЭ
 *
 * And step expects a specific answer:
 *
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidText(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat same step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ EMPTY, WHITESPACE, OR NULL INPUT
 ************************************************************
 * If incomingText.trim() is "":
 *
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidText(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat current step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ UNEXPECTED KEYWORDS (HELP, MENU, etc.)
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends:
 *     "help"
 *     "menu"
 *     "restart"
 *     "hello"
 *     "salam"
 *     "assalamualaikum"
 *
 * DURING any active step:
 *
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendUnexpectedKeywordReminder(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat SAME step
 *
 * MUST NOT:
 *     - Reset
 *     - Change step
 *     - Skip ahead
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ HALF ANSWERS (INCOMPLETE RESPONSES)
 ************************************************************
 * If step requires a sentence OR required fields:
 *
 * Example problem responses:
 *     - "donтАЩt know"
 *     - "maybe"
 *     - "?" 
 *     - partial message
 *
 * RULE:
 *   If answer does NOT meet minimal data requirement:
 *       тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidText(session)
 *       тЖТ Repeat same step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ MULTI-MESSAGE BURSTS (USER SENDS 2тАУ5 messages)
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends several messages back-to-back:
 *
 *   Only FIRST valid message should be processed.
 *
 *   All subsequent messages received before step reply:
 *       тЖТ MUST be ignored.
 *
 * Reason:
 *   Prevents step from auto-advancing twice.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ INVALID MEDIA WHEN MEDIA ALLOWED
 ************************************************************
 * If step allows optional media, but user sends:
 *     - corrupted file
 *     - unsupported MIME
 *     - broken URL from WhatsApp
 *
 * Then:
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidMedia(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat same step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 12 тАФ CASE UPDATE MODE PROTECTION
 ************************************************************
 * During existing case update:
 *
 *   If user sends command outside update menu:
 *       тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *       тЖТ Repeat update menu
 *
 * Update flow only accepts:
 *   - Option numbers
 *   - Valid media for upload step
 *   - Valid text for text-update step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 13 тАФ SESSION CORRUPTION PROTECTION
 ************************************************************
 * If ANY required session field is missing:
 *   - Preferred_Language
 *   - Flow_Type (after Step 2)
 *   - Current_Step_Code
 *
 * Auto-repair:
 *     session.Current_Step_Code = "LANG_SELECT"
 *     Session.save()
 *     return Texts.sendLanguageMenu(session)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 14 тАФ SURPRISE INPUT OUTSIDE EXPECTED FLOW
 ************************************************************
 * If message arrives when bot expects:
 *
 *     - A media file but receives text
 *     - A text answer but receives media
 *     - Numeric choice but receives paragraph
 *
 * THEN:
 *     тЖТ Send the appropriate validation message
 *     тЖТ Stay on SAME step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 15 тАФ CONTROL CHARACTERS, HTML, LINKS
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends:
 *     - URLs
 *     - HTML tags (<br>, <p>)
 *     - Control characters
 *
 * Treat as:
 *     тЖТ TEXT
 *
 * Apply normal step verification:
 *     If numeric required  тЖТ INVALID
 *     If yes/no required   тЖТ INVALID
 *     If free-text allowed тЖТ ACCEPT
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 16 тАФ OUT-OF-SCOPE CASES (NOT PART OF FLOW)
 ************************************************************
 * If user sends something the system cannot handle:
 *     - тАЬtrack my caseтАЭ
 *     - тАЬlocationтАЭ
 *     - тАЬcontact adminтАЭ
 *
 * And step is ANY question:
 *
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidText(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat same step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 17 тАФ HARD BLOCK DURING CASE SUBMISSION STAGE
 ************************************************************
 * During final submission steps:
 *
 *   ANY message OTHER than expected:
 *
 *       тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidText(session)
 *       тЖТ Repeat confirmation step
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 18 тАФ NON-SUPPORTED LANGUAGE MESSAGES
 ************************************************************
 * If user tries to send:
 *     - тАЬchange languageтАЭ
 *     - тАЬenglish pleaseтАЭ
 *     - тАЬurdu karoтАЭ
 *
 * AFTER selecting language:
 *
 *     тЖТ MUST NOT change language
 *     тЖТ Texts.sendUnexpectedKeywordReminder(session)
 *     тЖТ Repeat SAME step
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 18H тАФ SESSION TIMEOUT & INACTIVITY RULES (FINAL)
 *
 * Applies To:
 *    - Utils.gs  (Timestamp comparison logic)
 *    - Flows.gs  (Router тЖТ timeout handling)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *    Define EXACT rules for:
 *        - Detecting session timeout
 *        - Handling long inactivity
 *        - Repeating last question safely
 *        - Full reset on long-expired sessions
 *
 * NOTE:
 *    All timeout behavior MUST match the flowтАЩs official text:
 *
 *      тАЬтП│ Your session was inactive for a long time.
 *       I will repeat the last question.тАЭ
 *
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ SESSION TIMESTAMP RULE
 ************************************************************
 * Every time user sends ANY valid message:
 *
 *      session.Updated_At = NOW
 *      Session.save(session)
 *
 * This is the only timestamp used for timeout detection.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ TIMEOUT LIMIT (FLOW-DEFINED)
 ************************************************************
 * Flow defines timeout as тАЬlong inactivityтАЭ (12тАУ24 hours).
 *
 * Implementation constant:
 *
 *      TIMEOUT_HOURS = 24
 *
 * Router MUST check:
 *
 *      diffHours = (NOW - session.Updated_At) in hours
 *
 * If diffHours > TIMEOUT_HOURS:
 *      тЖТ Session considered TIMED OUT.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ TIMEOUT DETECTION LOGIC (Utils.gs)
 ************************************************************
 * function checkSessionTimeout(session):
 *
 *    const last = new Date(session.Updated_At).getTime();
 *    const now  = Date.now();
 *    const diffHours = (now - last) / (1000*60*60);
 *
 *    return (diffHours > TIMEOUT_HOURS);
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ TIMEOUT BEHAVIOR (Flows.gs)
 ************************************************************
 * When timeout is detected:
 *
 *    тЖТ DO NOT reset session.
 *    тЖТ DO NOT restart flow.
 *    тЖТ DO NOT send language menu again.
 *
 * Instead:
 *    тЖТ Texts.sendSessionExpiredReminder(session)
 *    тЖТ Repeat the LAST question EXACTLY.
 *
 * (User stays on SAME step without losing progress.)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ OFFICIAL MULTI-LANGUAGE TIMEOUT MESSAGE
 ************************************************************
 * EXACT text from the flow:
 *
 * English:
 *   тП│ Your session was inactive for a long time.
 *   I will repeat the last question.
 *
 * Urdu:
 *   тП│ ╪в┘╛ ┌й╪з┘Б█М ╪п█М╪▒ ╪║█М╪▒ ┘Б╪╣╪з┘Д ╪▒█Б█Т ╪к┌╛█Т█Ф
 *   ┘Е█М┌║ ╪в╪о╪▒█М ╪│┘И╪з┘Д ╪п┘И╪и╪з╪▒█Б ╪и┌╛█М╪м ╪▒█Б╪з █Б┘И┌║█Ф
 *
 * Roman Urdu:
 *   тП│ Aap kaafi dair inactive rahe.
 *   Main aakhri sawal repeat kar raha hoon.
 *
 * Hindi:
 *   тП│ рдЖрдк рдХрд╛рдлреА рджреЗрд░ рддрдХ рдирд┐рд╖реНрдХреНрд░рд┐рдп рдереЗред
 *   рдореИрдВ рдкрд┐рдЫрд▓рд╛ рд╕рд╡рд╛рд▓ рджреЛрдмрд╛рд░рд╛ рднреЗрдЬ рд░рд╣рд╛ рд╣реВрдБред
 *
 * Bangla:
 *   тП│ ржЖржкржирж┐ ржЕржирзЗржХржХрзНрж╖ржг ржирж┐рж╖рзНржХрзНрж░рж┐ржпрж╝ ржЫрж┐рж▓рзЗржиред
 *   ржЖржорж┐ ржЖржЧрзЗрж░ ржкрзНрж░рж╢рзНржиржЯрж┐ ржЖржмрж╛рж░ ржкрж╛ржарж╛ржЪрзНржЫрж┐ред
 *
 * Arabic:
 *   тП│ ┘Д┘В╪п ┘Г┘Ж╪к ╪║┘К╪▒ ┘Ж╪┤╪╖ ┘Д┘Б╪к╪▒╪й ╪╖┘И┘К┘Д╪й.
 *   ╪│╪г╪╣┘К╪п ╪е╪▒╪│╪з┘Д ╪з┘Д╪│╪д╪з┘Д ╪з┘Д╪г╪о┘К╪▒.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ REPEATING LAST QUESTION (MANDATORY)
 ************************************************************
 * After sending timeout reminder:
 *
 *    тЖТ Bot MUST resend the exact same question
 *        stored as `session.Current_Step_Code`.
 *
 * This ensures:
 *    - No flow loss
 *    - No step skipping
 *    - No data corruption
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ SESSION EXPIRY VS SESSION RESET
 ************************************************************
 * TIMEOUT (e.g., 24 hours):
 *      тЖТ do NOT erase session
 *      тЖТ keep all Temp_Data
 *      тЖТ keep Current_Step_Code
 *      тЖТ Simply repeat last question
 *
 * FULL EXPIRY / ABANDONED SESSION (7 days recommended):
 *      тЖТ If (NOW - Updated_At) > 7 days:
 *
 *            * Reset session completely
 *            * session = {}
 *            * Start from Step 1 (LANG_SELECT)
 *
 * This protects system from:
 *      - extremely old sessions
 *      - stuck flows
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ POST-TIMEOUT MESSAGE MUST NOT CHANGE FLOW
 ************************************************************
 * After timeout:
 *    - Do NOT adjust Flow_Type
 *    - Do NOT adjust region
 *    - Do NOT adjust Preferred_Language
 *    - Do NOT jump to next step
 *
 * User must resume EXACTLY where they left.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ MEDIA STEPS & TIMEOUT
 ************************************************************
 * If user timed out during a MEDIA-required step:
 *
 *      тЖТ Reminder message
 *      тЖТ Repeat photo/audio question EXACTLY
 *
 * Do NOT:
 *    - interpret timeout as failure
 *    - bypass required media
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ SPECIAL RULE: TIMEOUT DURING EXISTING CASE MENU
 ************************************************************
 * If timeout occurs while user is in:
 *      - Existing Case Menu
 *      - Case Status
 *      - Case Update Flow
 *
 * System MUST:
 *      тЖТ Send timeout reminder
 *      тЖТ Re-display the SAME menu or SAME question
 *
 * NO automatic exit.
 * NO automatic session reset.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ CONVERSATION RESUMPTION LOGIC
 ************************************************************
 * After timeout message is sent:
 *
 *   If user responds with ANYTHING:
 *       тЖТ Validate response normally
 *       тЖТ Continue flow normally
 *
 * No additional timeout checks needed.
 ************************************************************/

 * BLOCK 13 тАФ MASTER DATA STRUCTURE MAP (OFFICIAL)
 *
 * Based 100% on: Full n Final Flow Updated.txt

 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ USER_SESSIONS SHEET (SESSION ENGINE STORAGE)
 *
 * Purpose:
 *   Store the active user's temporary progress:
 *      - Region
 *      - Selected language
 *      - Which flow they are in (A/B/C)
 *      - What question they are currently answering
 *      - Temp data for answers before final case write
 *
 * Columns (EXACT as flow defines):
 *
 *   WhatsApp_Number
 *       - Sender's number (full international format)
 *       - Primary key to identify conversation
 *
 *   Current_Step_Code
 *       - Tracks exact step user is on:
 *           e.g., "LANG_SELECT", "USER_TYPE",
 *                 "A_Q1", "A_Q2", ..., "C_Q15"
 *
 *   Flow_Type
 *       - Set during STEP 2
 *       - Values:
 *           "A" тЖТ Searching for missing loved one
 *           "B" тЖТ User *is* the missing person
 *           "C" тЖТ Helping someone missing
 *
 *   Region_Group
 *       - Detected in STEP 0
 *       - Values:
 *           "PK", "IN", "BD", "ME", "OTHER"
 *
 *   Preferred_Language
 *       - Set after STEP 1
 *       - Allowed values determined by region
 *
 *   Temp_Data_Json
 *       - Stores all Q1тАУQ9 (Flow A),
 *         Q1тАУQ11 (Flow B),
 *         Q1тАУQ15 (Flow C)
 *       - Stores as JSON object until final write in STEP 4
 *
 *   Updated_At
 *       - Timestamp updated on every message
 *       - Used for inactivity/timeouts
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ CASES SHEET (FINAL CASE RECORD)
 *
 * Purpose:
 *   When user completes all questions in Flow A/B/C,
 *   STEP 4 writes ALL answers into a permanent case record.
 *
 * Columns (EXACT AS IN FLOW):
 *
 *   Case_ID
 *       - Generated in STEP 4
 *       - Format: CC-NNNNN  (e.g., PK-00001)
 *
 *   Created_At
 *       - Timestamp of case creation
 *
 *   WhatsApp_Number
 *       - Number that submitted the case
 *
 *   Region
 *       - UserтАЩs detected region at case time
 *
 *   Language
 *       - Selected Preferred_Language (from STEP 1)
 *
 *   Flow_Type
 *       - A / B / C
 *
 *
 * ******** FLOW A тАФ Q1 to Q9 (EXACTLY AS FLOW DEFINES) ********
 *
 *   Q1 тАФ Country of missing person
 *   Q2 тАФ Full name
 *   Q3 тАФ Age (approx allowed)
 *   Q4 тАФ Gender
 *   Q5 тАФ Last seen location (city/area)
 *   Q6 тАФ Last seen date/time
 *   Q7 тАФ Relationship with missing person
 *   Q8 тАФ Contact number for follow-up
 *   Q9 тАФ Photo (optional) тЖТ stored as Drive link(s)
 *
 *
 * ******** FLOW B тАФ Q1 to Q11 (EXACTLY AS FLOW DEFINES) ********
 *
 *   Q1  тАФ Origin country
 *   Q2  тАФ Full name
 *   Q3  тАФ Age (approx allowed)
 *   Q4  тАФ Original city/area
 *   Q5  тАФ Home location memory (landmark)
 *   Q6  тАФ How they got separated
 *   Q7  тАФ Who raised them
 *   Q8  тАФ Current location (city/area)
 *   Q9  тАФ Any remembered family names
 *   Q10 тАФ Contact number
 *   Q11 тАФ Photo (then & now) тЖТ Drive link(s)
 *
 *
 * ******** FLOW C тАФ Q1 to Q15 (EXACTLY AS FLOW DEFINES) ********
 *
 *   Q1  тАФ Where person was met
 *   Q2  тАФ When met
 *   Q3  тАФ Their full name
 *   Q4  тАФ Approximate age
 *   Q5  тАФ Gender
 *   Q6  тАФ Which country they belong to
 *   Q7  тАФ Which city/area they belong to
 *   Q8  тАФ Landmark memory
 *   Q9  тАФ How they got separated
 *   Q10 тАФ Who raised them
 *   Q11 тАФ Current country
 *   Q12 тАФ Current city/area
 *   Q13 тАФ Family member name remembered
 *   Q14 тАФ Contact number
 *   Q15 тАФ Photos (then & now) тЖТ Drive link(s)
 *
 *
 *   Extra_Notes
 *       - Any additional details provided by user
 *
 *   Media_Links
 *       - List of uploaded images/videos for case
 *
 *   Case_Status
 *       - Status visible in "Check Case Status" menu
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ CASE_UPDATES SHEET (FOLLOW-UP UPDATES)
 *
 * Purpose:
 *   Support "Existing Case" options:
 *     - Add info
 *     - Upload media
 *     - Mark case as resolved
 *
 * Columns:
 *
 *   Update_ID
 *       - Unique auto-increment for update record
 *
 *   Case_ID
 *       - The case being updated
 *
 *   Created_At
 *       - Timestamp of update
 *
 *   Update_Type
 *       - Possible values:
 *           "TEXT"     тЖТ Option 1 (New information)
 *           "MEDIA"    тЖТ Option 2 (Upload files)
 *           "RESOLVED" тЖТ Option 3 (Case marked resolved)
 *
 *   Content
 *       - Text typed by user (for TEXT updates)
 *
 *   Media_Links
 *       - One or more Drive links (for MEDIA updates)
 *
 *   Raw_JSON
 *       - Raw combined payload from WhatsApp:
 *           useful for debugging / traceability
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ DATA FLOW SUMMARY (STRICT FROM FLOW)
 ************************************************************
 *
 * STEP 1:
 *     тЖТ Store Preferred_Language in User_Sessions
 *
 * STEP 2:
 *     тЖТ Store Flow_Type in User_Sessions
 *
 * STEP 3A / 3B / 3C:
 *     тЖТ Save all Q1тАУQ16 answers into Temp_Data_Json
 *
 * STEP 4:
 *     тЖТ Create Case_ID
 *     тЖТ Write full row into Cases sheet (all Q answers)
 *     тЖТ Clear Temp_Data_Json
 *     тЖТ Mark session.status = "CASE_SUBMITTED"
 *
 * STEP 5:
 *     тЖТ Show Closing Message
 *     тЖТ Fully reset session
 *
 * EXISTING CASE LOGIC:
 *     тЖТ Does NOT modify main case unless Option 4 chosen
 *
 * UPDATE CASE FLOW:
 *     тЖТ Writes to Case_Updates sheet (1 row per update)
 *
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 14 тАФ MASTER STATE-CODE MAP (OFFICIAL)
 *
 * EXACT mapping of EVERY step тЖТ state code
 * EXACT transitions
 *
 * No additional states allowed.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * STEP 0 тАФ REGION DETECTION
 ************************************************************
 * (Not a user-facing state)
 * Occurs before any messages.
 *
 * No state code.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * STEP 1 тАФ LANGUAGE SELECTION
 ************************************************************/
LANG_SELECT
   тЖТ Transition:
        On valid option тЖТ USER_TYPE
        On invalid option тЖТ LANG_SELECT (repeat)




/************************************************************
 * STEP 2 тАФ IDENTIFY USER TYPE (A / B / C)
 ************************************************************/
USER_TYPE
   тЖТ Transition:
        1 тЖТ FLOW A тЖТ A_INTRO
        2 тЖТ FLOW B тЖТ B_INTRO
        3 тЖТ FLOW C тЖТ C_INTRO
        Invalid тЖТ USER_TYPE (repeat)




/************************************************************
 * FLOW A тАФ ELIGIBILITY CHECK
 ************************************************************/
A_INTRO
A_ELIGIBILITY
   тЖТ If тАЬNot eligibleтАЭ тЖТ A_REJECT
   тЖТ If eligible тЖТ A_Q1

A_REJECT
   тЖТ Options:
        1 тЖТ Restart тЖТ LANG_SELECT
        2 тЖТ End Chat тЖТ RESET




/************************************************************
 * FLOW A тАФ DATA COLLECTION (Q1тАУQ9)
 ************************************************************/
A_Q1  тЖТ A_Q2
A_Q2  тЖТ A_Q3
A_Q3  тЖТ A_Q4
A_Q4  тЖТ A_Q5
A_Q5  тЖТ A_Q6
A_Q6  тЖТ A_Q7
A_Q7  тЖТ A_Q8
A_Q8  тЖТ A_Q9
A_Q9  тЖТ A_CONFIRM




/************************************************************
 * FLOW A тАФ CASE CONFIRMATION
 ************************************************************/
A_CONFIRM
   тЖТ Confirm тЖТ CASE_SUBMIT
   тЖТ Invalid тЖТ A_CONFIRM




/************************************************************
 * FLOW B тАФ INTRO + QUESTIONS (Q1тАУQ11)
 ************************************************************/
B_INTRO
B_Q1   тЖТ B_Q2
B_Q2   тЖТ B_Q3
B_Q3   тЖТ B_Q4
B_Q4   тЖТ B_Q5
B_Q5   тЖТ B_Q6
B_Q6   тЖТ B_Q7
B_Q7   тЖТ B_Q8
B_Q8   тЖТ B_Q9
B_Q9   тЖТ B_Q10
B_Q10  тЖТ B_Q11
B_Q11  тЖТ B_CONFIRM




/************************************************************
 * FLOW B тАФ CASE CONFIRMATION
 ************************************************************/
B_CONFIRM
   тЖТ Confirm тЖТ CASE_SUBMIT
   тЖТ Invalid тЖТ B_CONFIRM




/************************************************************
 * FLOW C тАФ INTRO + ACCESS CHECK
 ************************************************************/
C_INTRO
C_INFO_SOURCE
   тЖТ If NO ACCESS тЖТ C_REJECT
   тЖТ If access тЖТ C_Q1

C_REJECT
   тЖТ Options:
        1 тЖТ Restart тЖТ LANG_SELECT
        2 тЖТ End Chat тЖТ RESET




/************************************************************
 * FLOW C тАФ DATA COLLECTION (Q1тАУQ15)
 ************************************************************/
C_Q1   тЖТ C_Q2
C_Q2   тЖТ C_Q3
C_Q3   тЖТ C_Q4
C_Q4   тЖТ C_Q5
C_Q5   тЖТ C_Q6
C_Q6   тЖТ C_Q7
C_Q7   тЖТ C_Q8
C_Q8   тЖТ C_Q9
C_Q9   тЖТ C_Q10
C_Q10  тЖТ C_Q11
C_Q11  тЖТ C_Q12
C_Q12  тЖТ C_Q13
C_Q13  тЖТ C_Q14
C_Q14  тЖТ C_Q15
C_Q15  тЖТ C_CONFIRM




/************************************************************
 * FLOW C тАФ CASE CONFIRMATION
 ************************************************************/
C_CONFIRM
   тЖТ Confirm тЖТ CASE_SUBMIT
   тЖТ Invalid тЖТ C_CONFIRM




/************************************************************
 * CASE SUBMISSION (COMMON FOR ALL FLOWS A/B/C)
 ************************************************************/
CASE_SUBMIT
   тЖТ Write to Cases Sheet
   тЖТ Transition тЖТ CLOSING_MSG




/************************************************************
 * STEP 5 тАФ CLOSING MESSAGE
 ************************************************************/
CLOSING_MSG
   тЖТ After sending message тЖТ RESET




/************************************************************
 * EXISTING CASE DETECTION (ADDITIONAL LOGIC)
 ************************************************************/
EXISTING_CASE_MENU
   тЖТ 1 тЖТ VIEW_CASE
   тЖТ 2 тЖТ CASE_STATUS
   тЖТ 3 тЖТ NEW_CASE (тЖТ LANG_SELECT)
   тЖТ Invalid тЖТ EXISTING_CASE_MENU

VIEW_CASE
   тЖТ Return to EXISTING_CASE_MENU

CASE_STATUS
   тЖТ Return to EXISTING_CASE_MENU




/************************************************************
 * UPDATE CASE FLOW
 ************************************************************/
UPDATE_CASE_SELECT
   тЖТ After selecting case тЖТ UPDATE_CASE_MENU

UPDATE_CASE_MENU
   тЖТ 1 тЖТ UPDATE_TEXT
   тЖТ 2 тЖТ UPDATE_MEDIA
   тЖТ 3 тЖТ UPDATE_RESOLVE
   тЖТ 4 тЖТ EXISTING_CASE_MENU
   тЖТ Invalid тЖТ UPDATE_CASE_MENU

UPDATE_TEXT
   тЖТ Save update тЖТ UPDATE_DONE

UPDATE_MEDIA
   тЖТ Save media тЖТ UPDATE_DONE

UPDATE_RESOLVE
   тЖТ Mark resolved тЖТ UPDATE_DONE

UPDATE_DONE
   тЖТ Return тЖТ EXISTING_CASE_MENU




/************************************************************
 * RESET STATE (SESSION END)
 ************************************************************/
RESET
   тЖТ Clear session
   тЖТ Next new message тЖТ LANG_SELECT
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 15 тАФ MASTER ROUTING BLUEPRINT (OFFICIAL)
 *
 * File:
 *   Flows.gs (Main Router)
 *
 * PURPOSE:
 *   Define EXACT step-by-step routing of messages through:
 *     - STEP 0 тЖТ STEP 5
 *     - Flow A / Flow B / Flow C
 *     - Existing Case & Update Case flows
 *     - All Additional Logic handlers
 *
 * NOTE:
 *   No extra states.
 *   No extra branches.
 *   Only what exists in Full n Final Flow Updated.txt.
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ MAIN ROUTER ENTRY (on each incoming message)
 ************************************************************
 * High-level sequence:
 *
 *   1) Load / create session (User_Sessions row)
 *   2) STEP 0 тАФ Region detection (if Region_Group empty)
 *   3) Check session timeout (Additional Logic 8)
 *   4) If no active flow тЖТ Existing Case detection (Additional Logic 1)
 *   5) Route by Current_Step_Code and Flow_Type
 *   6) Apply validation handlers (Additional Logic 3тАУ7)
 ************************************************************/

// PSEUDO-STRUCTURE (no new logic, only order):

function routeMessage(session, incomingText, mediaUrl, mediaMime) {

  /***** 1. REGION DETECTION (STEP 0) *****/
  // If Region_Group is not set:
  //   - Detect from WhatsApp number prefix
  //   - Store in session.Region_Group

  /***** 2. SESSION TIMEOUT CHECK (ADDITIONAL LOGIC 8) *****/
  // If (NOW - session.Updated_At) > TIMEOUT_HOURS:
  //   - Send Session Timeout message (all languages)
  //   - Repeat the last question (same step code)
  //   - Do NOT reset flow
  //   - Return

  /***** 3. EXISTING CASE DETECTION (ADDITIONAL LOGIC 1) *****/
  // If this number has submitted a case before:
  //   - Show Existing Case Menu instead of starting new case flow
  //   - Route inside Existing Case flows (see Section 6)

  /***** 4. LANGUAGE SELECTION / MAIN FLOW ROUTING *****/
  // Now route based on Current_Step_Code & Flow_Type:
  //
  //   - If no Preferred_Language:
  //        тЖТ STEP 1 тАФ LANGUAGE SELECTION
  //   - Else:
  //        тЖТ STEP 2 / 3A / 3B / 3C / 4 / 5
}




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ STEP 1 ROUTING тАФ LANGUAGE SELECTION
 ************************************************************
 * CONDITION:
 *   - session.Preferred_Language is empty OR
 *   - session.Current_Step_Code == "LANG_SELECT"
 *
 * ACTION:
 *   - Show region-based Language Menu:
 *       PK / IN / BD / ME / OTHER
 *   - User chooses one allowed language option.
 *
 * ON VALID INPUT:
 *   - Set: session.Preferred_Language = selected_language
 *   - Set: session.Current_Step_Code = "USER_TYPE"
 *   - Save session
 *   - Route тЖТ STEP 2 (Identify User Type)
 *
 * ON INVALID INPUT:
 *   - Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *   - Stay on "LANG_SELECT"
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ STEP 2 ROUTING тАФ IDENTIFY USER TYPE
 ************************************************************
 * CONDITION:
 *   session.Current_Step_Code == "USER_TYPE"
 *
 * ACTION:
 *   Show тАЬWho are you?тАЭ menu (region/language variants):
 *      1 тЖТ Searching for a missing loved one (Flow A)
 *      2 тЖТ I am lost / I am the missing person (Flow B)
 *      3 тЖТ I know someone who is missing (Flow C)
 *
 * ON VALID INPUT:
 *   If "1":
 *      session.Flow_Type        = "A"
 *      session.Current_Step_Code = (Flow A eligibility / intro)
 *      Route тЖТ STEP 3A
 *
 *   If "2":
 *      session.Flow_Type        = "B"
 *      session.Current_Step_Code = (Flow B intro / Q1)
 *      Route тЖТ STEP 3B
 *
 *   If "3":
 *      session.Flow_Type        = "C"
 *      session.Current_Step_Code = (Flow C intro / info-source)
 *      Route тЖТ STEP 3C
 *
 * ON INVALID INPUT:
 *   - Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *   - Stay on "USER_TYPE"
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ FLOW A ROUTING (STEP 3A)
 *     - Eligibility Check
 *     - Data Collection Q1тАУQ9
 *     - Route to STEP 4
 ************************************************************/

/*** 4.1 тАФ ELIGIBILITY QUESTION ***/
// CONDITION:
//   session.Flow_Type == "A"
//
// ACTION:
//   Ask: тАЬHas your loved one been arrested by the police
//          or any agency?тАЭ (multi-language)
//
// ON ANSWER "YES":
//   - Send region-language rejection text (Police/Agency)
//   - Show: тАЬWould you like to submit a new case?тАЭ
//         Options: 1 Yes / 2 No
//
//   If user selects "Yes":
//       - Return to STEP 2 (Identify User Type)
//   If user selects "No":
//       - End chat
//       - Reset session
//       - Send Final Closing Message (Police/Agency)
//
// ON ANSWER "NO":
//   - Proceed to Empathetic Intro (Flow A)
//   - Move to Q1тАУQ9 sequence


/*** 4.2 тАФ FLOW A QUESTION SEQUENCE (Q1тАУQ9) ***/
// After eligibility == "NO":
//
//   Show Empathetic Intro (all languages)
//   Then sequentially:
//
//     Q1 тЖТ Q2 тЖТ Q3 тЖТ Q4 тЖТ Q5 тЖТ Q6 тЖТ Q7 тЖТ Q8 тЖТ Q9
//
// Each answer:
//   - Stored temporarily (session / Temp_Data_Json)
//
// AFTER Q9:
//   - Save all answers to case record (for STEP 4 usage)
//   - Route тЖТ STEP 4 тАФ Case Confirmation
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ FLOW B ROUTING (STEP 3B)
 *     - User *is* the missing person
 *     - Q1тАУQ11
 *     - Route to STEP 4
 ************************************************************/

/*** 5.1 тАФ FLOW B INTRO + QUESTIONS ***/
// CONDITION:
//   session.Flow_Type == "B"
//
// ACTION:
//   - Show Empathetic Intro (all languages)
//   - Ask Q1тАУQ11 sequentially:
//
//     Q1 тЖТ Q2 тЖТ Q3 тЖТ Q4 тЖТ Q5 тЖТ Q6 тЖТ Q7 тЖТ Q8 тЖТ Q9 тЖТ Q10 тЖТ Q11
//
// Each answer:
//   - Stored temporarily
//
// AFTER Q11:
//   - Route тЖТ STEP 4 тАФ Case Confirmation
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ FLOW C ROUTING (STEP 3C)
 *     - Helper has access OR no-access
 *     - Rejection branch
 *     - Q1тАУQ15 branch
 *     - Route to STEP 4
 ************************************************************/

/*** 6.1 тАФ SOURCE-OF-INFORMATION QUESTION ***/
// CONDITION:
//   session.Flow_Type == "C"
//
// ACTION:
//   Ask:
//     тАЬDo you have direct access to the missing person,
//      or did you just see a post / hear about them?тАЭ
//
// OPTIONS:
//   1 тЖТ Yes, I have access
//   2 тЖТ No, I donтАЩt have access
//   3 тЖТ I belong to an organization where the missing person is present
//
// ON OPTION "2" (NO ACCESS):
//   - Send rejection message (No direct access)
//   - Show: тАЬWould you like to submit a new case?тАЭ
//         Options: 1 Yes / 2 No
//
//   If "Yes":
//       тЖТ Return to STEP 2 (Identify User Type)
//   If "No":
//       тЖТ End chat
//       тЖТ Reset session
//       тЖТ Send Closing Message (No-access rejection)
//
// ON OPTION "1" or "3":
//   - Proceed to Empathetic Intro (Flow C)
//   - Move to Q1тАУQ15 sequence


/*** 6.2 тАФ FLOW C QUESTION SEQUENCE (Q1тАУQ15) ***/
// After answer 1 or 3:
//
//   Show Empathetic Intro
//   Then sequentially:
//
//     Q1 тЖТ Q2 тЖТ Q3 тЖТ Q4 тЖТ Q5 тЖТ Q6 тЖТ Q7
//     Q8 тЖТ Q9 тЖТ Q10 тЖТ Q11 тЖТ Q12 тЖТ Q13 тЖТ Q14 тЖТ Q15
//
// Each answer:
//   - Stored temporarily
//
// AFTER Q15:
//   - Route тЖТ STEP 4 тАФ Case Confirmation
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ STEP 4 ROUTING тАФ CASE CONFIRMATION (COMMON A/B/C)
 ************************************************************
 * ENTRY CONDITIONS:
 *
 *   - Flow A:
 *       After Q9 of Flow A complete
 *   - Flow B:
 *       After Q11 of Flow B complete
 *   - Flow C:
 *       After Q15 of Flow C complete
 *
 * ACTION (as per flow):
 *
 *   On completion of all questions:
 *     - Generate Case ID (CC-NNNNN, e.g. PK-00001)
 *     - Save all collected answers into Cases sheet
 *     - Send region-language confirmation message
 *     - Set: session.status = "CASE_SUBMITTED"
 *     - Proceed to STEP 5 (Closing Message)
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ STEP 5 ROUTING тАФ CLOSING MESSAGE
 ************************************************************
 * TWO ENTRY PATHS:
 *
 *   1) After successful case submission (STEP 4)
 *   2) After rejection тЖТ user chooses "No"
 *
 * LOGIC (from flow):
 *
 *   IF user completed STEP 4:
 *       тЖТ Show Closing Message (all languages)
 *       тЖТ Reset session
 *       тЖТ End chat
 *
 *   IF eligibility / access rejection:
 *       IF user selects "No":
 *           тЖТ Show Closing Message
 *           тЖТ Reset session
 *           тЖТ End chat
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ EXISTING CASE MENU ROUTING (ADDITIONAL LOGIC 1)
 ************************************************************
 * TRIGGER:
 *   If system finds this WhatsApp number already has one
 *   or more cases in Cases sheet:
 *
 *   тЖТ Show Existing Case Menu instead of starting new case flow.
 *
 * MENU OPTIONS:
 *   1я╕ПтГг Review submitted case details
 *   2я╕ПтГг Check case status
 *   3я╕ПтГг Submit a new case
 *   4я╕ПтГг Update submitted case
 *
 * ROUTING:
 *
 *   If "1":
 *      тЖТ Review Case Details Flow
 *   If "2":
 *      тЖТ Check Case Status Flow
 *   If "3":
 *      тЖТ Start new Case Flow:
 *             тЖТ Return to STEP 2 (Identify User Type)
 *   If "4":
 *      тЖТ Start Update Case Flow (Additional Logic 2)
 *
 * MULTIPLE CASES:
 *   - Show list: {{CASE_LIST}}
 *   - User types desired Case_ID
 *   - If valid тЖТ route to selected flow (Review / Status / Update)
 *   - If invalid тЖТ send тАЬInvalid Case IDтАЭ and re-ask
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ UPDATE CASE FLOW ROUTING (ADDITIONAL LOGIC 2)
 ************************************************************
 * TRIGGER:
 *   User selects Option "4" in Existing Case Menu.
 *
 * STEPS:
 *
 *   1) Ask Which Case to Update (if multiple)
 *      - User enters Case_ID or "0" to go back.
 *
 *   2) Show Update Menu:
 *        1 тЖТ Add new information
 *        2 тЖТ Upload media
 *        3 тЖТ Mark case as resolved
 *        4 тЖТ Go back
 *
 *   3) ROUTING:
 *
 *        If "1":
 *           тЖТ Ask for new information text
 *           тЖТ Save update to Case_Updates sheet
 *           тЖТ Confirm submission
 *           тЖТ Show Closing Message (STEP 5)
 *           тЖТ End chat
 *
 *        If "2":
 *           тЖТ Ask for media (photo/video)
 *           тЖТ Accept multiple files
 *           тЖТ Save media links to Case_Updates sheet
 *           тЖТ Confirm submission
 *           тЖТ Show Closing Message (STEP 5)
 *           тЖТ End chat
 *
 *        If "3":
 *           тЖТ Mark case as resolved
 *           тЖТ Save update with type тАЬresolvedтАЭ
 *           тЖТ Confirm submission
 *           тЖТ Show Closing Message (STEP 5)
 *           тЖТ End chat
 *
 *        If "4":
 *           тЖТ Return to Existing Case Menu
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ ERROR, INVALID INPUT & EDGE-CASE ROUTING
 *       (USES ADDITIONAL LOGIC 3тАУ7)
 ************************************************************
 * APPLIES TO ALL STEPS:
 *
 *   - Menu steps (language, user type, existing case, update menu)
 *   - Question steps (Q1тАУQ15)
 *   - Media steps (photos, then & now)
 *
 * HANDLERS:
 *
 *   1) INVALID OPTION (menus)
 *        тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidOption(session)
 *        тЖТ Repeat same menu step
 *
 *   2) INVALID FREE TEXT (where meaningful text needed)
 *        тЖТ Texts.sendInvalidText(session, lastQuestion)
 *        тЖТ Repeat same question
 *
 *   3) PHOTO REQUIRED but not received (or wrong media)
 *        тЖТ Texts.sendPhotoRequired(session)
 *        тЖТ Repeat same step
 *
 *   4) VOICE NOTE received where text is required
 *        тЖТ Texts.sendVoiceNotAllowed(session)
 *        тЖТ Repeat same step
 *
 *   5) UNEXPECTED KEYWORDS (help, menu, start, etc.)
 *        тЖТ Texts.sendUnexpectedKeywordReminder(session)
 *        тЖТ Repeat same question
 *
 *   6) SESSION TIMEOUT (Additional Logic 8)
 *        тЖТ Texts.sendSessionExpiredReminder(session)
 *        тЖТ Repeat last question for same step
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 16 тАФ MASTER TEXTS STRUCTURE (OFFICIAL)
 *
