/************************************************************
 * LANGUAGE STRUCTURE RULE
 ************************************************************
 * EVERY Text block must contain SIX languages:
 *
 *   EN  тЖТ English
 *   UR  тЖТ Urdu
 *   RUR тЖТ Roman Urdu
 *   HI  тЖТ Hindi
 *   BN  тЖТ Bangla
 *   AR  тЖТ Arabic
 *
 * If a region does not allow some languages:
 *    тЖТ The menu file excludes them,
 *      but the underlying Text block MUST still contain
 *        all six language versions.
 ************************************************************/
/************************************************************
 * BLOCK 17 тАФ MASTER FUNCTIONS INDEX (OFFICIAL)
 * File: Flows.gs
 *
 * Purpose:
 *   List every function required by the flow:
 *      - Router
 *      - Step handlers
 *      - Flow A/B/C question handlers
 *      - Rejection handlers
 *      - Case confirmation
 *      - Existing Case logic
 *      - Update Case logic
 ************************************************************/




/************************************************************
 * 1 тАФ MAIN ENTRY POINT
 ************************************************************/

function routeMessage(session, msg, raw, mediaUrl, mediaMime)
    Purpose:
      - Central dispatcher for ALL incoming messages.
      - Picks correct flow based on session.Current_Step_Code.
      - Applies timeouts, region detection, and safety rules.
    Triggered:
      - Every incoming WhatsApp message.




/************************************************************
 * 2 тАФ STEP 0: REGION DETECTION
 ************************************************************/

function ensureRegionDetected(session)
    Purpose:
      - If Region_Group empty, detect region from phone number.
    Triggered:
      - Before ANY routing (only once per session).




/************************************************************
 * 3 тАФ STEP 1: LANGUAGE SELECTION
 ************************************************************/

function handleLanguageSelection(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Show region-specific language menu.
      - Validate user-selected language.
      - Set Preferred_Language тЖТ route to USER_TYPE.
    Triggered:
      - When Current_Step_Code = "LANG_SELECT".




/************************************************************
 * 4 тАФ STEP 2: USER TYPE SELECTION
 ************************************************************/

function handleUserType(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Show тАЬWho are you?тАЭ menu.
      - Set Flow_Type (A/B/C).
      - Route to correct flowтАЩs intro / eligibility step.
    Triggered:
      - When Current_Step_Code = "USER_TYPE".




/************************************************************
 * 5 тАФ FLOW A FUNCTIONS
 ************************************************************/

function handleA_Eligibility(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Ask eligibility question (police/agency).
      - If YES тЖТ send rejection path.
      - If NO  тЖТ go to empathetic intro + A_Q1.
    Triggered:
      - When Current_Step_Code = "A_ELIGIBILITY".


function handleA_RejectionOptions(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Decide between:
            1 тЖТ Restart (LANG_SELECT)
            2 тЖТ End Chat (Closing Message)
    Triggered:
      - When in "A_REJECT" state.


function handleA_Q(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Store answer to A_Q1тАУA_Q9
      - Move user to next A_Q step.
    Triggered:
      - When Current_Step_Code starts with "A_Q".


function handleA_Confirmation(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Show case confirmation message.
      - If confirmed тЖТ CASE_SUBMIT.
    Triggered:
      - "A_CONFIRM".




/************************************************************
 * 6 тАФ FLOW B FUNCTIONS
 ************************************************************/

function handleB_Q(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Store answer to B_Q1тАУB_Q11.
      - Move user step-by-step.
    Triggered:
      - When Current_Step_Code starts with "B_Q".


function handleB_Confirmation(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Show confirmation message.
      - If confirmed тЖТ CASE_SUBMIT.
    Triggered:
      - "B_CONFIRM".




/************************************************************
 * 7 тАФ FLOW C FUNCTIONS
 ************************************************************/

function handleC_InfoSource(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Evaluate тАЬDo you have access?тАЭ question.
      - Option 2 тЖТ Rejection.
      - Option 1/3 тЖТ Continue Flow C.
    Triggered:
      - "C_INFO_SOURCE".


function handleC_RejectionOptions(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Option 1 тЖТ Restart (LANG_SELECT)
      - Option 2 тЖТ End Chat (Closing Message)
    Triggered:
      - "C_REJECT".


function handleC_Q(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Store answers to C_Q1тАУC_Q15.
      - Auto-transition sequentially.
    Triggered:
      - States starting with "C_Q".


function handleC_Confirmation(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Show final confirmation.
      - If confirmed тЖТ CASE_SUBMIT.
    Triggered:
      - "C_CONFIRM".




/************************************************************
 * 8 тАФ CASE SUBMISSION (COMMON FOR A/B/C)
 ************************************************************/

function handleCaseSubmit(session)
    Purpose:
      - Write final data to Cases sheet.
      - Generate Case_ID.
      - Route to CLOSING_MSG.
    Triggered:
      - Current_Step_Code = "CASE_SUBMIT".




/************************************************************
 * 9 тАФ CLOSING MESSAGE
 ************************************************************/

function handleClosingMessage(session)
    Purpose:
      - Send final dua/closing message.
      - Reset session completely.
    Triggered:
      - "CLOSING_MSG".




/************************************************************
 * 10 тАФ EXISTING CASE DETECTION & MENU
 ************************************************************/

function showExistingCaseMenu(session)
    Purpose:
      - Present the Existing Case menu.
    Triggered:
      - When system detects previous cases.

function handleExistingCaseMenu(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Option routing:
          1 тЖТ View Case
          2 тЖТ Case Status
          3 тЖТ New Case
          4 тЖТ Update Case
    Triggered:
      - During Existing Case flow.




/************************************************************
 * 11 тАФ EXISTING CASE ACTIONS
 ************************************************************/

function handleViewCase(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Display stored case data.
    Triggered:
      - When user chooses тАЬReview case detailsтАЭ.

function handleCaseStatus(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Show Case_Status from Cases sheet.
    Triggered:
      - When user chooses тАЬCheck case statusтАЭ.




/************************************************************
 * 12 тАФ UPDATE CASE FLOW
 ************************************************************/

function handleUpdateCase_SelectCase(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - If multiple cases: select which Case_ID to update.
    Triggered:
      - "UPDATE_CASE_SELECT".


function handleUpdateCaseMenu(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - 1 тЖТ Add info
      - 2 тЖТ Upload media
      - 3 тЖТ Mark resolved
      - 4 тЖТ Back
    Triggered:
      - "UPDATE_CASE_MENU".


function handleUpdate_Text(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Add new text info to Case_Updates.
    Triggered:
      - "UPDATE_TEXT".


function handleUpdate_Media(session, mediaUrl, mediaMime)
    Purpose:
      - Accept photo/video.
      - Save Drive link into Case_Updates.
    Triggered:
      - "UPDATE_MEDIA".


function handleUpdate_Resolve(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Mark case as resolved тЖТ Case_Updates entry.
    Triggered:
      - "UPDATE_RESOLVE".


function handleUpdate_Done(session)
    Purpose:
      - Show completion message.
      - Return to main menu or end chat.
    Triggered:
      - "UPDATE_DONE".




/************************************************************
 * 13 тАФ SHARED SAFETY & REPAIR HELPERS (USED BY ROUTER)
 ************************************************************/

function repairMissingLanguage(session)
    Purpose:
      - If language lost/corrupted тЖТ force LANG_SELECT.

function repairMissingFlowType(session)
    Purpose:
      - If Flow_Type missing тЖТ return to USER_TYPE.

function repeatLastQuestion(session)
    Purpose:
      - After timeout or invalid input тЖТ re-send same Q.

function validateMediaForStep(session, mediaUrl, mediaMime)
    Purpose:
      - Enforce photo/audio/media rules based on step.

function validateNumericOption(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Check if input matches allowed numeric options.

function validateTextForStep(session, incomingText)
    Purpose:
      - Check free-text steps for invalid/empty input.
